character_event = {
	id = AVE_MARIA_opus_ruralium_commodorum_starting_pop.2
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_province = {
			limit = {
				has_owner = yes
				region = world_asia_minor
			}
			export_to_variable = { which = province_nb_settlement value = num_of_settlements }
			change_variable = { which = global_anatolian_settlement_nb which = province_nb_settlement }			
		}
		
		set_variable = { which = global_anatolian_pop value = 7079 }
		divide_variable = { which = global_anatolian_pop which = global_anatolian_settlement_nb }
	}
}
